<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасаться.html>спаса́ться</a> (7058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасать.html>спаса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spasátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасаться.html>спаса́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spasátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спастись.html>спасти́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to save oneself, to escape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасаться.html>спаса́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бегство.html>бе́гством</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spasátʹsja</b> bégstvom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flee; escape; run away</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасаться.html>спаса́йся</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spasájsja</b>, kto móžet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> every man for himself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to use as the thing that helps
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лекарство.html>лека́рством</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасаться.html>спаса́юсь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tólʹko étim lekárstvom ja i <b>spasájusʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this is the only remedy that helps</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасать.html>спаса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spasátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">спас-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spas-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***спасибо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a> (774)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier *<i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съпаси богъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭpasi bogŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ("save (you) God") (modern Russian: "<a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спаси́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a>"). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">спаси́бі</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spasýbi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spasíbo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thank you, thanks (for ... = <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <i>+ accusative case</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> (кому́-либо) <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> (komú-libo) za pómoščʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you (someone) for the help.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za sovét.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the advice.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za uslúgu/uslúgi.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the service/services.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ду</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za pobédu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the victory.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поддержка.html>подде́ржку</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za poddéržku.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the support.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимание.html>понима́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za ponimánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for understanding.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> сопережива́ние.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za sopereživánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the empathy.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оплата.html>опла́ту</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za oplátu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the payment.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщение.html>сообще́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za soobščénije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the report.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тыл.html>тыл</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za tyl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the (rear) support.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za cvetý.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thank you for the flowers.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Spasíbo</b> za to, što ty jestʹ u menjá!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thanks (for the fact) that I have you!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b>! / <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́е</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bolʹšóje <b>spasíbo</b>! / <b>Spasíbo</b> bolʹšóje!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Many thanks!; Thank you very much!</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Big thanks!</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***спасительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасительный.html>спаси́тельный</a> (7960)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спаситель.html>спаси́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spasítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасительный.html>спаси́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spasítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>saving, salutary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасительный.html>спаси́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможность.html>возмо́жность</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:шанс.html>шанс</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spasítelʹnaja</b> vozmóžnostʹ/šans</i> ― <span class="e-translation">heaven-sent opportunity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bringing salvation</li></ol>

***спасти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a> (1120)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съпасти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭpasti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ(n)</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pasti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pasture, herd</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасать.html>спаса́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to save, to rescue
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Chekhov</a>,  <cite>хори́стка</cite>  | <cite>The Chorus Girl</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средство.html>сре́дство</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нищета.html>нищеты́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позор.html>позо́ра</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A méždu tem jestʹ srédstvo <b>spastí</b> jevó i nas ot niščetý i pozóra.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And yet there is a chance of saving him and us from destitution and disgrace.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to salvage</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасти.html>спасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***спасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасть.html>спасть</a> (1265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасть.html>спасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спадать.html>спада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to abate, to fall <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to decrease or become less in strength</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеяться.html>наде́юсь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:жар.html>жара́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорый.html>ско́ро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спасть.html>спадёт</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nadéjusʹ, žará skóro <b>spadjót</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I hope the heat will <b>subside</b> soon.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасшийся.html>спа́сшийся</a> (7194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасшийся.html>спа́сшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spásšijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спастись.html>спасти́сь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spastísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***спать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a> (404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъpati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swep-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sleep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">soporific</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hypnosis</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">somnolent</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспать.html>поспа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sleep
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ložítʹsja <b>spatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have sex
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переспать.html>переспа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perespátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спаться.html>спа́ться</a> (15481)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спаться.html>спа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спаться.html>спи́тся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú ne <b>spítsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he can't sleep; sleep wouldn't come to him</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хорошо́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спаться.html>спи́тся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тро</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xorošó <b>spítsja</b> pod útro</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sleep is sound toward the morning</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***спекулировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спекулировать.html>спекули́ровать</a> (20579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">spekulieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спекулировать.html>спекули́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spekulírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">financial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to speculate, to profiteer, to gamble <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to exploit, to take advantage of</li>
<li>to speculate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***спекуляция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спекуляция.html>спекуля́ция</a> (14400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">speculatio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спекуляция.html>спекуля́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spekuljácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спекуляция.html>спекуля́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спекуляция.html>спекуля́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спекуляция.html>спекуля́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>speculation</li>
<li>scalping, profiteering, price gouging</li></ol>

***спелый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спелый.html>спе́лый</a> (8388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to ripen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спелый.html>спе́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spélyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)спеле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)спеле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ripe
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">The Quran, <i>19:25</i> :<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрясти.html>потряси́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ствол.html>ствол</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пальма.html>па́льмы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свежий.html>све́жие</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спелый.html>спе́лые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:финик.html>фи́ники</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">potrjasí na sebjá stvol pálʹmy, i popadájut na tebjá svéžije, <b>spélyje</b> fíniki</i></dd><dd>shake towards you the palm-tree's trunk and fresh, <b>ripe</b> dates will fall upon you</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***спереди.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спереди.html>спе́реди</a> (10496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спереди.html>спе́реди</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spéredi</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> from the front, at the front</li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="просторечное"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>прост</a>.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:передний.html>пере́дней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спереть.html>спере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sperétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">спира́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дыханье.html>дыха́нье</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спереть.html>спёрло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó dyxánʹje <b>spjórlo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it took his breath away</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сперматозоид.html>сперматозо́ид</a> (29077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сперматозоид.html>сперматозо́ид</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spermatozóid</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сперматозоид.html>сперматозо́ида</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сперматозоид.html>сперматозо́иды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сперматозоид.html>сперматозо́идов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spermatozoon</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спереть.html>спёртый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spjórtyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спереть.html>спере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sperétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спереть.html>спёртый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spjórtyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stuffy, close (poorly-ventilated; close)</li></ol>

***спеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a> (10381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">спѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spěti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hasten, to succeed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*spewd-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">press, hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">speed</i>. Akin to Slovene <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">speti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hasten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Slovak <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">dospieť</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grow mature</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Czech <span class="Latn" lang="cs">spět</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="cs">spěch</span>. Non-Slavic cognates include Sanskrit <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्फायते</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sphā́yatē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grow fat, increase</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">sich sputen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hasten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспеть.html>поспе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зреть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zretʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спец.html>спец</a> (13089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специалист.html>специали́ст</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">specialíst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спец.html>спец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спец.html>спеца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спец.html>спецы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спец.html>спецо́в</a></b>)

***специализация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:специализация.html>специализа́ция</a> (15101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специализация.html>специализа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">specializácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специализация.html>специализа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специализация.html>специализа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специализация.html>специализа́ций</a></b>)
